## intent:greet

- hello
- hi
- good morning
- good evening
- hey there

## intent:goodbye

- goodbye
- see you around
- see you later
- ciao

## intent:affirm
- yes
- indeed
- of course
- that sounds good
- correct

## intent:deny
- no
- never
- I don't think so
- don't like that
- no way
- not really

## intent:mood_great
- perfect
- very good
- great
- amazing
- wonderful
- I am feeling very good
- I am great
- I'm good

## intent:mood_unhappy
- sad
- very sad
- unhappy
- bad
- very bad
- awful
- terrible
- not very good
- extremely sad
- so sad

- are you a human?

- am I talking to a human?
- are you a robot?
